Based on java coding standards, "The switch statement should have the following form: Note there is no indentation for case clauses."
```suggestion
         switch (command) ``{``

         ...
         ``}``
```

### 43. DONO.. JIE `@xenthm` (11 comments)
</div>


<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/12#discussion_r1744720074" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**1 :fas-comment:**
</div>

I like the use of plural form of "word" to indicate an array of words!
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/12#discussion_r1744721587" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**2 :fas-comment:**
</div>

Not sure about this format, maybe you can refer to the Java coding standards document! I think it should be of the form:
```
if (condition) ``{``
    statements;
``}`` else if (condition) ``{``
    statements;
``}`` else ``{``
    statements;
``}``
```
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/12#discussion_r1744725294" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**3 :fas-comment:**
</div>

I like the use of `is` in the boolean `isCommand`! It makes it sound like a boolean. 
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/12#discussion_r1744726739" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**4 :fas-comment:**
</div>

I like that you attached the array specifier `[]` to the array type `Task` and not the array variable `storage`!
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/12#pullrequestreview-2281734272" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**5 :fas-comment:**
</div>

**Review Status:** COMMENTED

I think you did a good job with the coding standards overall! There is just one minor standard violation, but it doesn't change the readability of the code that much. 
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/85#discussion_r1744730321" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**6 :fas-comment:**
</div>

Not sure about this format for `switch` statements. I believe that it should be of the form: 
```
switch (condition) ``{``
case ABC:
    statements;
    // Fallthrough
case DEF:
    statements;
    break;
case XYZ:
    statements;
    break;
default:
    statements;
    break;
``}``
```

Note that `case` is on the same indentation level as `switch`. You can configure your IDE to automatically apply this format! Refer to Prof's lectures for the how-to. 
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/85#discussion_r1744731696" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**7 :fas-comment:**
</div>

Should `state` here be named a bit better to give readers and future developers an indication of what it does instead? I don't like how it is vague as of now. Since `state` can only take values from `[0, 1, 2]`, it might also be worth it to create an `enum` and some constants to indicate what each state means, to get rid of "magic numbers". 
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/85#discussion_r1744737462" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**8 :fas-comment:**
</div>

I like how you extracted single functions of the chatbot like listing all the tasks into their own method in the overall class! It helps greatly with modularity. 
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/85#discussion_r1744737683" expanded>
<div slot="header">

**9 :fas-comment:**
</div>

Perhaps you can change the filename and class name to `Lambo` to match the name you have given your chatbot!
</panel>

<panel  popup-url="https://github.com/nus-cs2113-AY2425S1/ip/pull/85#discussion_r1744738210" expanded>

According to the coding standards, The if-else class of statements would have the following form:
if (condition) ``{``
    statements;
``}``

Perhaps you could refactor your code? From
if (taskIndex == -1) return;

to

if (taskIndex == -1) ``{``
    return;
``}``
